--- Commit Message ---
LU-5896 mdt: allow release after blocking migrations

We now pass the new and old dataversion of the file after a blocking
migration to the kernel on the client to the MDS via an extension to
the MDS_SWAP_LAYOUTS RPC. Two data versions are added to the
mdc_swap_layouts part of this RPC.

These new fields are checked on the MDS only if the new flag
SWAP_LAYOUTS_WITH_DV12 is set in mdc_swap_layouts::msl_flags
which was previously set to 0 by the client, so no change in behavior
for old clients. Old servers will ignore the newly-added DV members in
the request as the structure doesn't contain it.

We can then transfer the new dataversion from the client
to the MDS through this extension. The MDD layer can
then update the dataversion accordingly on the server.

Add regression test sanity-hsm 607e.

Test-Parameters: testlist=sanity-hsm env=ONLY=607,ONLY_REPEAT=15

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2024-03-10 20:18:40.000000000) ---
Patch Set 22:

(10 comments)

It looks like there are still some wire protocol data structures that are being modified but do not have existing checks.  It would be best if those had checks added to wirecheck.c/wirestest.c *before* this patch was landed, to avoid any protocol issues with this patch.

Note that it is possible to increase the size of RPC buffers without breaking interoperability, so that would probably be better in the long run than adding a separate buffer for just MDS_SWAP_LAYOUTS_DV.  

However, I'm not sure what your compatibility requirements are for this?  Have you already deployed this change on your own systems using the extra RPC buffer?

--- Message (Guillaume Courrier, 2024-03-11 10:07:40.000000000) ---

For the compatibility requirements, we only have used this patch in a test setup, not a production environment yet so modifications are ok. If I understand what you are saying correctly, I can add a field at the end of the RMF_SWAP_LAYOUTS field (struct mdc_swap_layouts) as long as the server is capable of differentiating old and new clients with the mls_flags field that already exists?

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2024-03-11 10:17:43.000000000) ---
Patch Set 22:

> By "before this patch was landed" do you mean adding those checks
 > in a seperate patch below this one for the fields that existed
 > before or adding them here would be ok?

It would be best if it was done in a separate patch, which could be pushed directly to master to preserve the pre-existing struct/constant values.  Then this patch can be rebased on top of it, but the wiretest patch can test/review/land independently.

 > For the compatibility requirements, we only have used this patch in
 > a test setup, not a production environment yet so modifications are
 > ok. If I understand what you are saying correctly, I can add a
 > field at the end of the RMF_SWAP_LAYOUTS field (struct
 > mdc_swap_layouts) as long as the server is capable of
 > differentiating old and new clients with the mls_flags field that
 > already exists?

Exactly correct.  The nodes can also check the buffer size, but using flags is better.
